id='comparison-with-other-engines'>Comparison with Other Engines</h1> <p>We compared Gunrock against several other engines for graph analytics:</p> <ul> <li><a href="https://developer.nvidia.com/nvgraph">nvGRAPH (GPU)</a></li> </ul> <p>Below are comparative results on 5 primitives times 9 datasets in terms of graph throughput (millions of edges per second,
